## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task belongs to population ecology, where the growth rate dP_dt is typically modeled as a function of the current population P and possibly time t. Classical growth models (logistic, Gompertz, Allee effect, etc.) describe how population change depends on density and environmental factors.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P
- Logistic growth (differential form): dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P)
- Allee effect (bistable): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (c2 - P)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P**c2)
- Ricker-like density feedback: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * P) - c2 * P
- Seasonally forced exponential: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t + c3))
- Time-varying carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t) - P)
- Saturating growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P / (c1 + c2 * P)
- Linear growth with immigration: dP_dt = c0 + c1 * P
- Decaying growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) + c2 * P
- Power-law time dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * t)
- Seasonal logistic with harvest: dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 - P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) - c4 * P

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Constant per capita growth rate ŌåÆ dP_dt proportional to P
- Linear decrease in per capita growth with density ŌåÆ dP_dt = P * (c0 - c1 * P)
- Logarithmic density dependence ŌåÆ per capita growth proportional to log(carrying capacity / population) (Gompertz)
- Sigmoidal population trajectory ŌåÆ differential equation with quadratic or higher polynomial in P
- Bistable population thresholds ŌåÆ cubic polynomial in P with three fixed points (Allee effect)
- Seasonal forcing ŌåÆ multiplicative periodic function of t (sin, cos) in growth rate or carrying capacity
- Density-dependent growth with exponent ŌåÆ per capita growth rate = c0 - c1 * P**c2 (theta-logistic)
- Exponential density dependence ŌåÆ per capita growth rate proportional to exp(-c * P) (Ricker-like)
- Decaying growth over time ŌåÆ dP_dt includes factor exp(-c * t) or power-law t^{-c}
- Migration/immigration effects ŌåÆ constant additive term in dP_dt independent of P
